<h2 class="kt-adv-heading1718_d5469f-b8 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-1-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading1718_d5469f-b8">About Danni in The Desert</h2>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column1718_a34cba-cb"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<div class="wp-block-media-text is-stacked-on-mobile is-vertically-aligned-center" style="grid-template-columns:45% auto"><figure class="wp-block-media-text__media"><img decoding="async" width="598" height="600" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20598%20600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="" class="wp-image-10786 size-full" data-lazy-src="https://dannibindubai.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/Danni-image-598x600.png"/><noscript><img decoding="async" width="598" height="600" src="https://dannibindubai.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/05/Danni-image-598x600.png" alt="" class="wp-image-10786 size-full"/></noscript></figure><div class="wp-block-media-text__content">
<p></p>



<p class="has--font-size">Hey! I&#8217;m Danni 🙂</p>



<p class="has--font-size">I&#8217;ve called Dubai home since 2013, leaving behind my family and friends in the UK. I&#8217;ve lived in JLT, Downtown Dubai and Jumeirah.<strong> I&#8217;ve experienced Dubai both as a resident and tourist,</strong> first as a <strong>solo female</strong> and later as a <strong>mum with a toddler</strong> in tow!</p>



<p class="has--font-size">Which is why I decided to create this website to share all my insider knowledge that you won&#8217;t find anywhere else!</p>



<p class="has--font-size"><strong>Helping you avoid the common challenges</strong> that come with visiting or living in Dubai.</p>



<p class="has--font-size">Over the years, I&#8217;ve seen a lot of misconceptions about Dubai. So I&#8217;m also passionate about <strong>breaking stereotypes of Muslims and Dubai</strong>.</p>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns1718_6d26c7-fb"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn1718_9abd28-3e kt-btn-size-standard kt-btn-width-type-auto kb-btn-global-fill kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false  wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://dannibindubai.com/about-me"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text">Find out the BIGGEST misconceptions</span></a></div>
